***долго.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> (276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Adverb for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dólgij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dólgo</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-до́лго" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)до́льше</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-до́лго" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-до́лго" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>доле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a long time; for a long time
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приказать.html>приказа́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On prikazál <b>dólgo</b> žitʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He died</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">He ordered you to live long</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The adverbs <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dólgo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, along with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">да́льше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dálʹše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, follow imperfective verbs.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долговой.html>долгово́й</a> (18744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolg</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долговой.html>долгово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dolgovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> debt

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:долговой.html>долгова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьма́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dolgovája</b> tjurʹmá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">debtor's prison</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>debt</b> prison</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***долголетие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долголетие.html>долголе́тие</a> (26224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долголетие.html>долголе́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dolgolétije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долголетие.html>долголе́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долголетие.html>долголе́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долголетие.html>долголе́тий</a></b>)
</p>

***долгосрочный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгосрочный.html>долгосро́чный</a> (14960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dólgij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">srok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Probably a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">langfristig</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долетать.html>долета́ть</a> (12527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долетать.html>долета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долететь.html>долете́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(to, as far as)</i>, <i>(thrown object, projectile etc)</i> to reach</li>
<li>to reach
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долетать.html>долета́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>кри́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do nas <b>doletáli</b> kríki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sound of shouting reached us [our ears]</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долетать.html>долета́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обрывок.html>обры́вки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do nas <b>doletáli</b> obrývki razgovóra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we could hear fragments of the conversation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***долететь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долететь.html>долете́ть</a> (9341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долететь.html>долете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doletétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долетать.html>долета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(to, as far as)</i>, <i>(thrown object, projectile etc)</i> to reach
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долететь.html>долете́ть</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>doletétʹ</b> (do céli)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall short (of)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́ца</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смочь.html>смогла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долететь.html>долете́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ptíca ne smoglá tudá <b>doletétʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the bird could not fly that far</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:долететь.html>долете́ли</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak vy <b>doletéli</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> did you enjoy your flight?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reach</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долженствующий.html>долженству́ющий</a> (29834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долженствующий.html>долженству́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dolženstvújuščij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:должностной.html>должностно́й</a> (12002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:должность.html>до́лжность</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dólžnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:должностной.html>должностно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dolžnostnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> office, duty, position <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">job</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:должностной.html>должностно́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dolžnostnóje</b> licó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">official, functionary, officeholder</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>office</b> person</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:должностной.html>должностно́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:преступление.html>преступле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dolžnostnóje</b> prestuplénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">malfeasance, misconduct (in office)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>office</b> crime</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dólžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:должность.html>до́лжность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dólžnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:должность.html>до́лжности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:должность.html>до́лжности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:должность.html>должносте́й</a></b>)

***долина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:долина.html>доли́на</a> (3089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dolina</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dolъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ina</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долина.html>доли́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dolína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долина.html>доли́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долина.html>доли́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долина.html>доли́н</a></b>)
</p>

<li>vale, dale</li></ol>

***доложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доложить.html>доложи́ть</a> (2051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доложить.html>доложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:докладывать.html>докла́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to report, to announce <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to notify formally</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to add more, to put more (e.g. into a portion)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>до́ля</a> (2075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dòľa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>до́ля</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dólja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>до́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>до́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>доле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>part, portion, share</li>
<li>fate, lot</li></ol>

***дом.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> (100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*domъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house; home</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dom</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́мы</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>домо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>house <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">building</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обыскивать.html>обы́скивать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́мом</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obýskivatʹ <b>dom</b> za <b>dómom</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to search house by house</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>home</li>
<li>family</li>
<li>household</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The nominative-accusative plural <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́мы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dómy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, largely unused now, was in earlier Russian (as late as 19th century) sometimes restricted to the accusative case and distinguished from a nominative plural <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">domá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare the nominative plural <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">домовє</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">domove</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, accusative plural <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">домꙑ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">domy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> of Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">домъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">domŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dóma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шний</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domášnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домовый.html>домово́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домой.html>домо́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домовладелец.html>домовладе́лец</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domovladélec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">домосе́д</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domoséd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***домашний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шний</a> (1680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-šnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">domášnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>home, household, house</li>
<li>private</li>
<li>domestic; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> family
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шнее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>domášneje</b> živótnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">domestic animal; pet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>home-made, homespun</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домовый.html>домово́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домовый.html>домо́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домовитый.html>домови́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">domovityj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">domášnij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шнего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шние</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шних</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (own) folks, family</li></ol>

***доминировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доминировать.html>домини́ровать</a> (19211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">dominieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доминировать.html>домини́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dominírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to prevail, to predominate</li>
<li>to command, to dominate</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:домишко.html>доми́шко</a> (15434)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dom</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ишко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-iško</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(pejorative suffix)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домишко.html>доми́шко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">domíško</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домишко.html>доми́шка</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домишко.html>доми́шки</a><sup>1</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домишко.html>доми́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домишко.html>доми́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a (small) house</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:домкрат.html>домкра́т</a> (28723)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">dommekracht</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домкрат.html>домкра́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">domkrát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домкрат.html>домкра́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домкрат.html>домкра́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домкрат.html>домкра́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jack (device for raising and supporting a heavy object)</li></ol>
